[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1619[0m[39m:        len_remain = [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint32_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1620[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mind && [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen_remain == [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen - [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1621[0m[39m:            [0m[35m/[0m[39m* new buffer received so adjust length and indefinite flag *[0m[35m/[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1622[0m[39m:            len -= [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1623[0m[39m:            end_offset -= [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1624[0m[39m:            ind = false;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1625[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen_remain < len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1626[0m[39m:            [0m[35m/[0m[39m*[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1627[0m[39m:             * error - short frame, or this item runs past the[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1628[0m[39m:             * end of the item containing it[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1629[0m[39m:             *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1630[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mber_add_large_length_error[0m[1;39m([0m[39mactx->pinfo, tree, tvb, offset, len, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlen_tvb, len_offset, len_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1631[0m[39m:            return end_offset;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1632[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1633[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1634[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1635[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1636[0m[39m:    actx->created_item = NULL;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1637[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1638[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpc[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1639[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* constructed *[0m[35m/[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1640[0m[39m:        end_offset = [0m[1;35mreassemble_octet_string[0m[1;39m([0m[39mactx, tree, hf_id, tvb, offset, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlen, ind, out_tvb, nest_level[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1641[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1642[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* primitive *[0m[35m/[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1643[0m[39m:        int length_remaining;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1646[0m[39m:#if [0m[1;36m0[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The stack underflow stems from the reverse-copy loop in the BER string parsing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroutines [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnotably in `dissect_ber_constrained_octet_string_impl` and its [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrestricted/constrained-string variants[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. These functions compute a write pointer [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`buf_end = buf + max_len`, then decrement it once per byte of BER content, without [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecking that the BER length [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`len`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m does not exceed the buffer capacity. When `len[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m> max_len`, the first `*--buf_end` underflows one byte before `buf`, corrupting the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mredzone of the `name_string` in the caller.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Core Logic to Preserve[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The reverse-copy approach [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwriting characters from the end of the BER string [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minward[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is used to produce a null-terminated, reversed or direct string for [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisplay. When the BER string length fits within the buffer, the current logic must [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremain unchanged.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The null terminator at the end of the copied string must still be written [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexactly once.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing BER length checks [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., against the TVB length and sentinel [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecks for large lengths[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m should remain intact.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Strategy[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Locate all occurrences of reverse-copy loops in packet-ber.c. Search for the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern “*--buf_end” in functions:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `dissect_ber_constrained_octet_string_impl`[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `dissect_ber_constrained_restricted_string`[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Any similar helper implementing reverse-copy for BER string types [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mGeneralString, PrintableString, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. In each such function, replace the unbounded reverse-copy loop with a [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounds-clamped version:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      i.  Determine the buffer capacity:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            size_t buf_capacity = max_len;        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m maximum bytes including [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mterminator[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ii. Compute the number of bytes to copy:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            size_t copy_len = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen < buf_capacity - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? len : buf_capacity - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          This ensures room for `copy_len` bytes plus a null terminator.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      iii.Initialize the write pointer:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            char *write_ptr = buf + copy_len;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      iv. Perform the reverse-copy safely:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            for [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t i = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < copy_len; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                write_ptr--;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                *write_ptr = [0m[1;35mget_next_byte_from_tvb[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m - i[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      v. Null-terminate:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            buf[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mcopy_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      vi. [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptionally[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m If `len > buf_capacity - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`, record or flag a truncation, or[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msilently drop the excess bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mconsistent with other string dissectors[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Example Pseudocode Patch [0m[1;39m([0m[39min `dissect_ber_constrained_octet_string_impl`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m existing variables: uint32_t len;  int max_len;  char buf[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mmax_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      size_t buf_capacity = max_len;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      size_t copy_len = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen < buf_capacity - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? len : buf_capacity - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      char *write_ptr = buf + copy_len;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      for [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t i = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < copy_len; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          write_ptr--;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          *write_ptr = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_guint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, copy_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m - i[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      buf[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mcopy_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Repeat analogous changes in `dissect_ber_constrained_restricted_string` and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39many other reverse-copy routines.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Harness and Tests[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No modifications to fuzzing harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`fuzzshark.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or test code.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The public API and dissection semantics remain unchanged for all valid-length [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstrings.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Only strings exceeding the buffer now truncate safely, avoiding overflows.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Large BER strings will be truncated to `max_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` bytes. This is an [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39macceptable display-time limitation; Wireshark routinely truncates long fields in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissectors.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If desired, add an `expert_info` warning tree item when truncation occurs, but[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis is optional and should not block the patch.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No performance impact on normal-sized strings; only a small branch to compute [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`copy_len`.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Clamping the copy length before pointer arithmetic directly eliminates the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderflow without altering the overarching dissection logic.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar patterns exist in other Wireshark dissectors [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., PrintableString[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich already enforce `len <= buffer_size - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` before writing.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach isolates the fix to the specific string-processing code, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavoiding global changes or modifications to utility functions.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
